<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanranding.html>aanranding</a> (12958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanranden.html>aanranden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:assault.html>assault</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:abuse.html>abuse</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ation, -ing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:development.html>development</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> specifically “sexual assault” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> informed <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanranding.html>aanranding</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerbaarheid.html>eerbaarheid</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwen.html>aanschouwen</a> (12411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenschouwen</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">aan-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schouwen.html>schouwen</a></i>.
